  const OPEN_NAV = 'nav[data-framer-name="Phone Open"], nav[data-framer-original-name="Phone Open"]';
  const isMobile = () => window.matchMedia('(max-width: 1024px)').matches;

  function clickLikeUser(el) {
    try { el && el.dispatchEvent(new PointerEvent('pointerdown', {bubbles:true})); } catch {}

  }

  function hardHide(nav) {
    if (!nav) return;
    const prev = {
      pe: nav.style.pointerEvents,
      op: nav.style.opacity,
      ds: nav.style.display
    };
    nav.dataset._prev = JSON.stringify(prev);
    nav.style.setProperty('pointer-events', 'none', 'important');
    nav.style.setProperty('opacity', '0', 'important');
    nav.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important');
    // libera depois para permitir reabrir
    setTimeout(() => {
      try {
        const p = JSON.parse(nav.dataset._prev || '{}');
        nav.style.pointerEvents = p.pe || '';
        nav.style.opacity = p.op || '';
        nav.style.display = p.ds || '';
      } catch {}
      delete nav.dataset._prev;
    }, 500);
  }

  function closePhoneMenu(fromEl) {
    const nav = (fromEl && fromEl.closest(OPEN_NAV)) || document.querySelector(OPEN_NAV);
    if (!nav) return;

    // 1) botão “X” (Icon)
    const icon = nav.querySelector('[data-framer-name="Icon"]');
    if (icon) { clickLikeUser(icon); return; }

    // 2) às vezes o toggle está no wrapper do topo (“Name”)
    const nameWrap = nav.querySelector('[data-framer-name="Name"]');
    if (nameWrap) { clickLikeUser(nameWrap); return; }

    // 3) toggler com aria-expanded
    const toggler =
      document.querySelector('button[aria-expanded="true"], [aria-controls][aria-expanded="true"]') ||
      nav.querySelector('button[aria-expanded="true"], [aria-controls][aria-expanded="true"]');
    if (toggler) { try { toggler.click(); } catch {} return; }

    // 4) overlay/backdrop comuns
    const overlay =
      nav.querySelector('[data-overlay], [data-framer-name*="Overlay"], .framer-overlay, .backdrop, .overlay') ||
      document.querySelector('[data-overlay], [data-framer-name*="Overlay"], .framer-overlay, .backdrop, .overlay');
    if (overlay) { try { overlay.click(); } catch {} return; }

    // 5) Fallback visual
    hardHide(nav);
  }

  // Dispara fechamento AO TOCAR num link do menu (antes do navegador navegar)
  function onLinkDown(e) {
    if (!isMobile()) return;
    const target = e.target;
    if (!target) return;

    // aceita <a href="#...">, <a href="./#...">, <a href="./eua#...">
    const anchor = target.closest && target.closest('a[href]');
    if (!anchor) return;

    const href = anchor.getAttribute('href') || '';
    // Só age se o clique vier de DENTRO do menu aberto
    const nav = anchor.closest && anchor.closest(OPEN_NAV);
    if (!nav) return;

    // Considera como link de navegação/âncora (mesmo com prefixo ./ ou ./eua)
    const isAnchorNav = href.includes('#');
    if (!isAnchorNav) return;

    // fecha o menu imediatamente (sem impedir a navegação/rolagem)
    closePhoneMenu(anchor);
  }

  // Cobrir iOS/Android e desktop pequeno: pointerdown + touchstart + mousedown, em CAPTURA
  document.addEventListener('pointerdown', onLinkDown, { capture: true });
  document.addEventListener('touchstart', onLinkDown, { capture: true });
  document.addEventListener('mousedown', onLinkDown, { capture: true });

  // Se a URL mudar para âncora (ex.: /eua#start), garanta que esteja fechado
  window.addEventListener('hashchange', () => {
    if (!isMobile()) return;
    const nav = document.querySelector(OPEN_NAV);
    if (nav) closePhoneMenu(nav);
  });

})();
</script>

    <!-- End of bodyEnd -->
</body>
</html>
